Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Selected Words
103
Rev. Sun Myung Moon's Words Compilation Committee

Preface
                   President of the World Peace Unification Family Association, Hwang Seon-jo

1)
The Bell of the Heart
Now you all said, "Happy New Year," but why did you say that? 
"Today is the first day of the lunar calendar." (Interpreter) Ah, I see. "How did you know? (Interpreter)" Hmm. How did you know? (Laughter) In China, Korea, and Japan, we have used the lunar calendar since ancient times. Nowadays, we also use the solar calendar, but Eastern people believe they become a year older only after the lunar year passes. So you also need phrases like "Happy New Year." (Laughter) 
Humans Shine Like Light Bulbs
Alright, today let's talk under the title "The Bell of the Heart." When you climb a high mountain at night or fly in an airplane and look at the city, you see many lights. If there are blue or red lights, they stand out. If there is a big light among them, it stands out even more. Similarly, when viewed from the spiritual world or by God, we often think that humans are the same. 
Now, the human heart represents humanity. No one exists without a heart. People are centered around their hearts. If that heart is like a light, then there must be a bulb, and inside it, there must be a filament. Both inside and outside must be equipped. "Are you talking about lights? (Interpreter)" Yes, that's right. In terms of electric lights, there must be a bulb, and inside it, there must be a filament. 
Now, the fact that such a bulb shines light does not come from the bulb itself. We think about how it is connected through power lines to a power plant that is not visible. If the bulb is large and has a high capacity, the wire must be thick. When you turn on the switch, electricity must flow in and the light turns on. 
So where is that electricity? Is it inside the bulb? That's the question. When the light comes on, it is in the bulb, but it is also everywhere that is connected. This logic holds. If you ask someone who knows nothing about electricity, "Where is the electricity?" they will say, "It's in that switch. The electricity is there." But where is the fundamental source? It is in the power plant; it is only connected to the power plant. 
If you go to the power plant, you will see a large mass of metal turning to provide electric light. That's right. Hydroelectric power has conduits that channel water to utilize large waterfalls. Then, thermal power must transport coal via a conveyor, burn it to produce steam, and turn turbines. Usually, people studying under electric lights or looking at electric lights don't think about this. They just think that way. Isn't that so? "That's right." In this view, the farther the power line is, the more effort has gone into it. We come to think that many sacrifices have been made. 
When you look at that small bulb, if it breaks, it becomes useless, and if the tungsten filament breaks, it also becomes useless. You keep feeling that. The breaking of a light bulb is like a person dying. Similarly, if the filament inside, like the heart, breaks, it is the same. In this way, you will eventually think that you will shine as a human being like a light bulb, that you will exist. 
Humans Desire Light That Cannot Be Followed
So, how many volts can you fit into a bulb? Is it a small fixed bulb or a large one? What about you? "It's big." How many watts? "It's infinite." You say it's infinite, but do you really believe that? (Laughter) 
Therefore, have you thought about how many watts of light can be connected behind you? The wire must be thick. So you should feel, "It's heavy; I can't carry this." Have you felt that way? So, the thicker it is, the more bulbs of tens of thousands or hundreds of millions of watts can be connected. The wire and socket must be there, and it must be set up so that bulbs can always be replaced in that socket. 
When you think this way, you cannot help but consider what position you are in if we compare humans to sockets or bulbs. What do you think? When you look at this, the entire process of humans being born and growing up is like replacing bulbs or sockets. It is like preparing to make the wire thicker and the socket larger to install high-wattage electric lights. 
Now, is that an easy task? "No." Is it expensive or cheap? (Laughter) Those who say, "Oh, I can just sit comfortably and look at the light," are not concerned, but to truly stand in that position is indeed a difficult task. 
You try to boast about that small light. "This is me, me, me. This is it." If there is a bulb worth a thousand watts and you turn it on here, does this (small light) have any use? It is of no use. Whether it exists or not is the same. Rather, it is cumbersome and an obstacle. Isn't that so? "That's right." When thinking of that, God must have thought the same way. So God created the sun in this universe. He created a light that cannot be followed. Just one sun is enough. 
The reason we need electricity is that there is night and there are shadows. That is why it is needed. Isn't that so? So do you need electricity or sunlight? "Sunlight." Why? Because there is nothing beyond that. No matter how many bulbs you have, under sunlight, they are all useless. 
We Must Ring the Bell of the Heart Like Pure Gold
When we look at the human world, we sometimes say "the light of the heart." Have you heard such a phrase? Is there such a phrase in English? Is there no phrase like "the lamp of the heart"? How poetic is that? "The light of the heart, the light of the heart" can be said like that. Similarly, what is today's title? It is "The Bell of the Heart." So what is the bell? It is to announce. It is a signal. Among the sounds of bells, there are good bell sounds and bad bell sounds. That's right. 
Then, if you look at yourselves, if you compare your hearts to fire, they are like bulbs, and if you compare them to sound, you can say you have something like a bell. No matter how much you need electric light, you must connect to the socket, and no matter how many bells there are, they must be rung. 
You all have hearts, right? "Yes." Who rings the bell of your heart? Do you know your heart is functioning? "Yes." Huh? Are you sure you know? "Yes." The heart reacts by saying "That's good!" when something good happens, and "You rascal!" when something bad happens. Is that true? "Yes." 
When we look at it centered on the heart, you have hearts, but your ancestors also had hearts. If you go back to your ancestors' ancestors' hearts... if you go all the way up, there must be some God at the center of this universe, and there must be a heart of God, right? "Yes." 
Then how is God's heart different from your hearts? Huh? Would it be different or the same? "Different." "The same." Think about that. Do you think they are the same or different? "The same." Then do you all resemble God? (Laughter) It is like electricity. If God is the power plant, you are like a light bulb. That is undeniable. 
The electricity must be well exchanged between plus and minus. The two must become one. They must be completely united. Even though there are two eyes, the degrees of the two eyes must match well. They must enter the optic nerve and align well at the focal angle. The same goes for the ears. If one hears strongly and the other weakly, that won't do. (Pointing to the ears) They must hear together. The frequencies and waveforms must be the same. If one nostril is blocked, is that good? (Blocking one nostril while speaking. Laughter) 
Thus, the less obstruction there is, the brighter the light. If there is no obstruction, it becomes the same as the electric quantity of the original power plant. To be the same, the consumed part, in terms of electricity, is called resistance, and there must be no resistance. This resistance consumes electricity. You are the same. Is your body and heart united like pure gold, or are they like a piece of wood? There are many series from pure gold to pure silver, pure copper, pure iron, and so on. There are countless series. 
So what does electricity desire? It desires everything to be pure gold. Pure gold is like a taut wire. It absolutely dislikes wood and stone. So when a person allows electricity to flow through their heart, the bell rings. The bell of the heart rings. If that bell is one hundred percent pure gold and perfect, God will hear that bell sound for thousands of years and say, "Ah! That's good." You all ring the bell of the heart. Each will ring it in their own way. Some will have broken bells, ragged bells, and all sorts of bells. There are people who live without knowing whether their bell is broken or malfunctioning. What about you? "……." What about those who are dozing off? (Laughter) Even when electricity comes, there is no sound, just "Hmm! Beep!" 
The Sage Rings the Pure Bell of Truth
When we look at it this way, it is undeniable that you live your whole life ringing the bell of the heart. Centered on this, there will be someone who rings it in your village, someone who rings it in your town, and someone who rings it in the army; they will all be different. It is the same at home. In the home, if there is a righteous person, a trustworthy person, when they say, "Let's do this," everyone listens. Everyone listens. Even if it is the father, if he does something wrong, he can be told, "No." When comparing the bell of my heart with the father, if I am right, I can say, "Ah, that won't do." 
However, throughout the long historical era, countless people have come and gone. The question is how much of a bell they have made. The question is how much they have rung that bell. 
From this perspective, all the knowledge, philosophy, religion, and everything that is called the truth of reality today is an expression that arises from the heart. It is all an expression of the heart. If it is pure, global, and historical, it must be preserved in the museum of that country. 
From this perspective, who are the people we can remember in the history of humanity today, or whom we commemorate in history? They are the ones who have rung the pure bell of truth. So what remains historically? It is not the one who was strong. It is not the one who had a lot of money. It is not the one who was a powerful nation. Those things all pass away. 
When we look at it this way, the saints who remain in history are those who have rung the bell of truth that represents several centuries or thousands of years in the historical era. Because that bell sound is good, everyone imitates it and gathers, saying, "I am good too. I am good too," forming a cultural religious sphere. 
To Teach True Life, Character, and Love, One Must Teach the True God
Then among the religious people, who would be the true saints? Think about that. What should saints teach? They must teach true life and true character. Then they must teach true love. It is not just about people; they must also teach about the true character of God. 
When you look at saints, they are all religious leaders. They are the masters of the bell. Isn't that so? "Yes." Why is that? Because they taught new ideals centered on eternity, transcending history, and they taught about the God who provides all ideals above history. That is why people gather in that religion. 
Now, temporary people, those who live with life as their goal, all flow away. This is the same in the animal world. But only humans are different; they want to live eternally. Eternal life is not for the wicked but for the true. This principle ultimately emerges. 
In your country, they reported yesterday that Rockefeller died, and if that person were true, the reaction would be greater. If Rockefeller were a true person, the American people would say, "Oh, even if our country disappears, that person should have lived." Look at that. Rockefeller was the vice president of the United States, and there is no one in America who does not know him, yet when he dies, people say, "He died, so what?" But Jesus, who died on the cross two thousand years ago, still has many people remembering and weeping for him. What a difference that is! 
So what is different? What is different? Is the human form different? The appearance is all the same. What is different? What is different? The heart is different. The heart. All teachings that manifest as a reaction of the heart are in this world.
This was for the universe, for history. 
When viewed this way, people think about history and eternal life, not just for ten or a hundred years, but for a thousand, ten thousand, or even millions of years. When a person dies, they are like an animal; what remains after that? Nowadays, even those who do not believe in religion or do not know God think, "Ah, I must leave a legacy." But what is the point of leaving a legacy? Even if you become a patriot of America and have a memorial, when America falls, all those memorials will be destroyed. Only the American people will know... What does it matter to leave a name? Therefore, in the era of history where rise and fall occur, no matter how much you leave behind, it will eventually be treated poorly.

However, every sovereign lives less than a hundred years and dies, and countries do not last for hundreds or thousands of years before they fall. But what if there is someone who never dies or falls? If such a being exists, you would want to entrust and rely on everything you have left behind, including your name and honor, to that being. Don't you think so? 

If there is a God who must meet the counterpart, then that God is such a being. He is the master of history, the master of the existence world, and the subject who manages everything eternally. Because of this existence, our hearts operate with the nature of wanting to entrust and leave things under His management. We must leave something behind.

Then, do we need money? "No." That is just one of the things in this world, one of the possessions. It is not something particularly precious. However, a person must be reborn anew.

Then why have the saints become the light of humanity's heart today and the source of gathering all people? When looking at this issue, it is because they discussed eternity and unchangeability.

Such saints exist in the East and here, and there are many. There are four great saints. Among these saints, who is the center? "Jesus." Why? Why is it Jesus? "Because He is the Messiah." Who recognized Him as the Messiah at that time? They killed the Messiah, and now we call Him the Messiah; was He the Messiah then? Who acknowledged Him as the Messiah? In that era, He was probably not as famous as Reverend Moon. (Laughter) So why is He the greatest among the saints? You need to understand that. First of all, He said, "I am the only begotten Son." What does the only begotten mean? It means the person who monopolizes God's first love.

You will all get married and have children, but raising the first child is something extraordinary when you love that first child. Do you think so? "Yes." Those who are not married can think, "That would be the case." (Laughter) But what about God? God is the same. It is the same. Therefore, Jesus received 100% love, and He had the mindset that the branches of love would first extend to the world of humanity through Him.

Then what will the only begotten do? Is only the man the only begotten? Where is the woman? Where did the only begotten daughter go? At the same time that Jesus thought of Himself as the only begotten, He thought of the only begotten daughter. Although it is not in the Bible, it is the same story. That way, women would not protest. American women, especially strong-minded women... (Laughter) It is true, but it is also a fact.

If God exists, and if God is a God of love, then if there is a begotten son, there must be a begotten daughter for it to be recognized that "Ah, God is fair." (Applause from women) God does not prefer to have only one leg; He likes to have both legs. (Laughter) So Jesus thought, "I am the only begotten, so I must find the only begotten daughter." Because He could not find the only begotten daughter, He said while dying, "When will the bridegroom come to find the bride?" That was all He did in His life.

Today, Christians say that everyone, even men, is "the bride before the Lord." How can a man be a bride? What, does the church become the bride? Where is there such a thing as the church becoming the bride? What does it do with Jesus? If the church is the bride, will Jesus touch her hand, kiss her, or love her? What is the use of that? (Laughter) Perhaps the presidents of your countries do not know how to kiss? "No." If there are famous presidents or kings in the world, should they not know how to kiss or love? "No."

Then, Jesus, the King of Kings, is there a law that says, "The King of Kings must be a bachelor"? "No." Then He must have a counterpart, right? Would the King of Kings, Jesus, sit on His throne and teach, "It is better for you to live alone like me," or would He say, "It is better for you to live together"? What would He say? "He would say it is better to live together." Otherwise, the church is a crippled church. It is a crippled king. That is why saying that Jesus must get married is fundamentally reasonable, yet Reverend Moon says this, and they call it heresy.

Now, would Jesus like Reverend Moon saying, "Jesus must get married," or would He prefer someone saying, "Jesus should not get married"? Think about it from Jesus' perspective. What would it be? Who is Jesus' son? "God." He is the Son of God. Then who made the man? "God." Who made the woman? "God." What did God make the man and woman for? "To become one." Yes, He said to live together as one. That is the most sacred thing. It is the most sacred.

God did not just create Adam and say, "It is good." He created Eve as well and said, "It is good." Why? Because both God and Adam and Eve are good, He said it is good. If only God is good and Adam and Eve are not, then it is not good. Until now, many religions, including Christianity and Buddhism, live a single life, but the Unification Church says, "Living a single life is a sin." It is different. (Applause)

Then what did Jesus say? He saw this world as a world of Satan and said there is nothing to find in this world. He said that no matter how good the sounds are in this world, there is nothing worth listening to. As the only begotten, He thought about the only begotten daughter, the only begotten family, and the only begotten nation; He thought all that way. It is different. Do you understand? "Yes." That is why He can be recognized as the center among the saints. (While writing on the board)

Recognized as the center among the saints, Jesus
Today, everyone is asserting themselves, and even among the saints, they fight and assert, "You are not the center; I am the center." Isn't that so? It can happen. Even among you, you do not want to lose to each other, right? Even little kids, like these kids.

Then who must recognize that? No matter how much the saints recognize each other, it is not enough. If there is a central God who can oversee the saints, then that being, God, must recognize it.

If God recognizes it, but it does not match His heart, will He recognize it just to stop the fighting? Therefore, it must be recognized. It is because it is a fact that the center is determined. For God to endorse it, there must be something that can make God fall head over heels, and that is love. (While writing on the board)

God does not need money, knowledge, or power; He needs none of that. 

Among the men born as humans, when Jesus said, "Before You, I am the only begotten Son," this statement resonated deeply in God's ears. It pleased Him. God must have thought, "You are the only begotten? Humanity that believed in God as Father for four thousand years; are you saying you are the greatest among them? Are you greater than Moses of Judaism or Abraham?" Jesus must have said, "Yes, yes." Then God asked, "How will you prove that to me?" Jesus would have replied, "Whatever you do, I will do. They can oppose heaven and betray, and they can change a thousand or ten thousand times, but I will never change, even for millions of years. I am absolute."

Centered on the thought of the only begotten, even if you cut this, it does not change; even if you cut something bigger, it does not disappear; even if you cut something larger, it does not vanish. If you cut it in half, the only begotten divides into two; if you cut it into ten, the only begotten divides into ten, but it does not change. Thus, if you cut off a finger, you do not curse, saying, "God, why did you cut this off?" Instead, you say, "I am your only begotten. This only begotten's hand was cut off for you." 

There is no candidate who can compete with that. There cannot be a presidential candidate like in an election. It is absolute. The concept of Jesus is absolute; it is absolute. No one can think they can be a candidate for His position. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." There has never been such a person until now. There has also never been such a woman. What about you nowadays? Huh? In your eyes, do you only see people with money or those who are talented? Do you go looking for such people? "No." What do you mean no? It is true, but you cannot help it, so you say no. (Laughter) You are being wishy-washy. You should be straightforward. You are being all over the place, right? 

When you bless someone, do you think, "Oh, if I do this with that person, it will be a blessing, but I would rather retreat"? You think like that, right? "No." 

Then, if Jesus is the only begotten, would He be a talented person or an untalented person? Would He be a foolish person or a clever person? Think about it. Is Jesus a foolish person or a clever person? (Laughter) What that means is that even if you cut this one thing, even if you cut a finger at the joints, it is absolute. "I am definitely the only begotten, the only begotten. Even if you cut one cell, I am still the only begotten. This determination and this pride is that I am the greatest." That is what He thought. "God, just give me a command." If He gives a command, He will do anything. He will do anything. Do you understand? "Yes."

In that sense, Jesus is the only begotten. Among the saints, there is no other saint who can claim to be the greatest based on love except Jesus. He did not say to make this world better; He did not fundamentally try to overturn it. He did not try to fundamentally reform it. Other saints did not try to fundamentally reform it. They managed some countries well and did this or that, but they did not deny that it was fundamentally wrong and did not try to start anew centered on God's love.

What Jesus said was, "What I know is only between God and me." That is what He said. "Now, I will create the only begotten daughter who can love God with my hands." That is what He meant. Then, He would give birth to sons and daughters, create a new family, a new lineage, a new nation, a new state, and a new world.

The only thing that can be boasted before God is the achievement of love.
It was only during Jesus' time that this sound of a bell rang out. That is why this ringing sound did not only move the earthly world but also moved God's heart and God's love. It was able to ring the bell of God's heart loudly. God was not displeased with the bell that Jesus rang; He was pleased. Why? Because it was the sound of love. (Laughter, applause) Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

What would God like? Would He like life? God is eternal and the source of all life, so He does not need it. Knowledge? God is the king of knowledge and the subject of knowledge. Power? He is the great power that moves this vast universe. Money? God does not need money either.

So what does He need? Look at what God needs. Does He need food? Does He need anything? Does He need a house? "No." What does He need? "Love." Why? What does God do with love? Huh? Why does God like love? Huh? God also wants to get intoxicated, to get intoxicated. (Laughter, applause) So what does God want? It is to be intoxicated with love.

It is not just that He says, "Oh, this is good. Ha ha ha!" He is so pleased that He dances with joy. This love is not just something that can be sung and danced about; it is something beyond that. He forgets all His dignity and face and simply enjoys it. Even if God says that this is the best, if the whole world does it, who can criticize it? "No one." In love, there is no high or low, no wide or narrow, no big or small; they are all one. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."

So, if you say to God, "I have given a lot of offerings, so please let me succeed," then God will take you to the heaven filled with gold and treasures and say, "You little brat, look around here." What you have given is not even worth a piece of tissue paper. Then, if you boast about what you have done for God, it is nothing compared to the restoration providence that God has carried out until now; it is just a speck of dust. Does that make sense? There is nothing to boast about. "Please recognize me. Please bless me and send me to heaven." Do you have the qualifications for that? You do not.

So, everything you boast about before God, whether you have suffered a lot or have a lot of gold and treasures, when you look for it, there is nothing that says you loved. There is no love, no love. There is nothing that says God loved, that God was pleased, that you loved centered on God's love.

What is the limit of that love? It is a love that can love humanity beyond Satan, beyond any king of your parents or your country. The sign that God ultimately triumphed, the sign that everything is fulfilled, is concluded when that love is found. It is concluded; everything is. There is nothing beyond that.

So what is all humanity doing now? They are all competing. They are competing. They are competing to see who can truly love centered on this love. Korea and America are competing, white people and people of color are competing; everyone is competing.

God does not look at money or culture. He looks at love. Because He sees through the glasses of love, He does not see anything other than love. Everything is invisible. Everything is nonexistent. Therefore, God wants love to shine as brightly as that electric light, like an electric light.

So, do you love God? "Yes." Do you love Reverend Moon? "Yes." You are unsure about whether to love Reverend Moon, but do you love God? You are unsure about whether to love God, but when you love, it will change, but do you love God? You say you love Reverend Moon, but is that love genuine, or is it just words? Do you love Reverend Moon?
"How, how? Do you know what kind of relationship Reverend Moon has with God? 'Son of God.' How do you know if I'm lying? How do you know if he's the Son of God or the Son of Evil? How do you know if he's Satan? 'Because I love.' Even if you say you love, how many have deceived women on the street claiming to love them? How do you prove it, how? How do you know? How do you know? How do you know if I'm wrong? How do you know if Satan has influenced this? (Laughter) It's simple. I love, so it's okay to hit me or say whatever. It's all good. (Cheers. Applause) If that's true, then you would say, 'It's okay if you insult me and kill me. What can I do if I am good?' That's real love. Is that right? 'Yes.' (Laughter. Applause)

So when you look at the Bible, Jesus said, 'My God, why have you forsaken me?' He made a fuss about it, but I think that's absolutely not good. It should be removed. If at that moment he had said, 'I have come from you, I have inherited your love, and for your love, I will walk this path in glory,' how wonderful would that have been? Do you understand what I mean? 'Yes.'

So, even if the teacher goes to prison, he does not pray. He does not pray in difficult times. 'The place I am in is the place of family, but what you want is to sacrifice the family to find the tribe, so I will sacrifice my family to find our tribe. Today, people from all over the world, from various races, have come to the Unification Church, so I will sacrifice them to liberate humanity and at the same time liberate the spiritual world.' That is the prayer he makes. God is bound to humanity, so to release this, humanity must be liberated. Only then can God be liberated. Do you understand? 'Yes.'

You must have true love for God to occupy heaven. In this view, throughout human history, countless people have rung their own bells and lit their own lamps, but among them, what is the sound of the bell that can cover the world and remain forever, and what is the light that can shine forever? Knowledge? Truth? No. It is love. It is the sound of true love's bell. Depending on how much of this you have, whether you occupy heaven and God's world is determined, and depending on how broadly you connect this, your authority in the heavenly kingdom is determined.

Now, our Unification Church members are fundraising and working hard for a purpose, but they say, 'Even though I work so hard for the Unification Church, they don't recognize me and don't love me.' I think like this. Reverend Moon says, 'I will put all my effort into making money and will offer everything, even if I go into debt many times over.' What about offerings? Tithes? What is tithing? It means putting everything in. 'When I go to the heavenly kingdom, I will offer all my sincerity for God, and even if I owe the most to Rockefeller or the Bank of America, I will work for God.' That is the kind of thinking I have.

So, when God sees, 'Hey, you fool, can't you think? How long do you think you will live in this world? Shouldn't you take care of yourself?' Would He say that? 'No.' Then would He praise or scold? 'He would praise.' On such days, when I do things while in debt, He gives me back several times what I owe. He prepares several times in advance. When I am in trouble because I have no money, God directly commands and provides through unexpected people. Do you understand? Do you get what I mean? 'Yes.'

Then, even if thousands of small bells ring, when the big bell sounds, all those sounds disappear. That is the sound of the bell centered on love. In your homes, the sound of the bell centered on love shines brighter and is better. That sound is good 24 hours a day, whether you are sleeping, awake, during the day, or while eating. It is always good. There is no place where it is not welcomed, transcending time, and there is no time or place where it is not welcomed.

Those girls didn't know love. (Laughter) They don't know love. They are dull to love.

Today's message is titled 'The Sound of the Heart's Bell.' What does that mean? You all say, 'Oh! When it comes to home church, it's a bit better when the teacher tells us to do it, but Mr. Park is making it hard for us to do home church.' Isn't that right? 'No.' Even if the teacher is strict and Mr. Park is unpleasant to see, those who carry the lamp of love and the sound of love in their hearts are the ones who win.

When you do home church, the people you interact with will be drawn to that love, and if they don't see you, they will want to see you, so when evening comes, they will prepare food to keep you from leaving, and you will see an environment where they want to spend the night having fun. You should see that kind of environment. So even when it becomes twelve o'clock and dawn arrives, even though the night is bright, they will be so drunk that they won't let you go, and they will wish that this moment would last forever. You should see that kind of situation.

A World in Confusion and Despair  
Everyone, you know that since the First World War, we have been living in a world of confusion, a continuous era of war. This historical course has not occurred by chance; it is a path of indemnity history that humanity must go through, based on the vast history of human affairs, which we have learned from the principles.  
All intellectuals around the world are saying that we are in a rapidly changing world. With such rapid change, where will we go? Ordinary people see a high risk of reaching a world of despair with such rapid changes. Very few believe that we will reach a world of hope. The Western civilization that has led modern civilization has not only fallen but is said to have already entered a night world. The Christianity that has been the spiritual pillar of Western civilization, and families, societies, and nations centered around Christianity have all tilted to the point of collapse.

God’s Will and Us
We, the people gathered in the Unification Church, are not gathered because of anyone’s will, but we are gathered because of God’s will.
God’s will includes everything.
When we talk about "God’s will," it includes everything, as you know. It includes me, my family, my nation, the East and West, and the entirety of this earthly world and the spirit world.
God’s will is all interconnected and relates to form one path. However, in our human world, there are many people, people from various nations. There are men and women, older people and younger people, all kinds of people. And there are people from various professional fields, such as the arts, literature, philosophy, and various social strata. Now, you all too, you all. No matter where you are led, you will go. If you quietly observe and it’s wrong, you may not know, but if it’s wrong, it’s a big deal, but if you think it won’t be wrong, hold on and go until your life is exhausted. “Yes!” (Applause) 
Then, look. Reverend Moon is now 60, so he will soon go to the spirit world. When you go to the spirit world and see, “Where did the teacher go? Where did the teacher go?” What do you think it will be like? Who will you look for? If you die in your sleep and morning comes, who will you look for? “Father.” Father. Father is at the bottom of hell, at the bottom of hell. So what will you do? Because you love everyone, because you love, you will go even to the bottom of hell for love. You will go to hell. So everywhere you go is the bottom of hell. It’s all hell, but then you open the door to the very bottom of hell, sit down, and greet, and it turns out to be the kingdom of heaven. (Cheers and applause) 
So how much…. I say, “Oh Reverend Moon, where have you gone?” “Why! I’m here.” “Yes.” Going to hell and then going to heaven is much more thrilling than just going to heaven, isn’t it? (Applause) When you ask how this happened, the answer is, “Those who have love turn hell into heaven.” That’s the answer. (Cheers) Love is better than freedom! “Yes.” So I love that. That is love. (Applause) 
Proclaim the Unification Church globally 
Thus, I have accomplished 95 percent. You all, the teacher has traveled around the world, receiving all kinds of criticism, and has proclaimed our Unification Church globally. In the 1970s, it was judged to be at the peak in the world. Was the teacher’s word right or wrong? Did it remain in America or not? “It remained.” 1978 was the most difficult time. Was it or not? “It was.” The day we win, the communist party will all be broken. Then what about Deng Xiaoping…. The name Deng means “to rise,” and Xiaoping means “to spread small.” So this has become a disgrace. The name is good. When China came here and invaded Vietnam, how much disgrace spread? All the prestige has been shattered. 
So what about Carter? The American President Carter means “cut.” In the end, America will fall, it will fall to communism, it will fall to communism, it will fall, that’s how it is. The name is like that. (Laughter) Huh? Everything I said is happening. 
It was just yesterday that 1978 passed. Huh? “Yes.” That’s why for three years, 1979, 80, 81, if you all push hard, everything will fly far away. (Clapping) Then when you say “bang” globally, it will have an impact beyond opposition. Then you must fill the gunpowder and then harden the bullets and push them in. 
Then is a short barrel good or a long barrel good? “A long one.” Why? Why? If those guns can reach 20 li and have bombs at the end, isn’t that ideal? (Laughter) Reverend Moon has thought about that. You all think, “Oh! How can we make that?” How can we make it? God can make it. Imagine you are firing such a gun. If you hesitate, you will be in big trouble. If the day comes when you can’t shoot, everyone…. You will also die. You will also go. 
So there is that danger, so I have explosive power in myself. The switch goes bang! And then in the second round too. Do you understand what I mean? “Yes.” If you just stand anywhere, go back! Go back! Go back! (Laughter) Then in one shot, it all ends from here. 
Do you want to fire thousands of rounds? “Yes.” If you do it your way, you could shoot for millions, billions of times and die of old age without dying. Because it shoots randomly, it shoots randomly…. So inevitably, you must fix it in place to shoot straight. What comes next? After going through the family era, you will go through the tribal era, the national era; you all know that. You must know that. Why? If you don’t know that, all your strength will be wasted. Because you know that, you go all the way. Do you understand? 
You all, think about it, if I dig a sewer pipe and break through a thousand-mile path, how great would that be? You must break through quickly, even through floods. Even if your ears fall off and your legs fall off, you want that; would you go out alone like that? You need that. 
Let’s govern heaven and earth and return home 
Now, do you understand clearly? “Yes.” Do you want to take a thousand years to return home, or one year? “One year.” Instead, no matter how much your legs fall off, the goal is God’s love. It’s the heart, the heart. That is how it is twisted. Does it seem like it should disappear? “Yes.” “Oh, I’m hungry, oh, I’m cold, oh, I’m miserable, oh, this girl is twenty-five years old, what is this?” Will you say that? “I will endure.” Yes, you must think that way. All at once, whoosh. It’s the same. You all started this time, but if you don’t do this well for a few years and say, “That’s how it is,” you won’t be able to go even after millions of years. 
Now, why did Reverend Moon come to America and cause problems to unite? What is the need for the Washington conference, what is the need for the Yankee Stadium conference, what is the need for the Madison Square Garden conference? So what is the need for “wangwangwang…”? What is the need for that? Reverend Moon, respected in the religious world, Reverend Moon in the business world, Reverend Moon in the cultural world, it’s all Reverend Moon, Reverend Moon. He is a person who influences American culture, someone you can’t remove. This organization is structured like this, and in a short time, laying the foundation like this, my way of doing things, you can’t find it anywhere else. Do you know why? Bullets must be fast and strong to penetrate. They must break through. They break through the whirlpool of American culture. 
I am surrounded by American culture, and I am doing this; did I break through? “You broke through.” So smart you all are sitting here for three hours. You don’t even realize your back hurts. When you sit in church, after just 40 minutes, you feel like you’re going to die, but you’re doing this. (Laughter and applause) 
Here, you all have one thing to learn. You all, representing the family of Adam and Eve in the Garden of Eden, must love here. This is what you do. (Writing on the board) How much did you truly love? Love humanity as you love God, all of it. Show everything Reverend Moon has done here. So the 95 percent that Reverend Moon has created, this is all given to you by God and Reverend Moon. It’s a promise, a promise. So even the brief imitation of opposing here, though it doesn’t last long, must be gone through. 
Thus, you will all be recognized as those who can govern heaven and earth and return to your hometown. This is how you return home. So when you say, “Ah! The 95 percent I inherited from Reverend Moon is the global condition for restoration, and I have combined the 5 percent condition to make a 100 percent condition and have come to find your heart of love,” God will say, “Ah, you came, well done.” Satan will also say, “Hmm, well done.” Why? Even though he opposed and did all sorts of things, he will say, “He is a person who is not related to the opposing world.” Then God will say, “Amen,” and you will also say, “Amen,” and even though Satan dislikes it, he will say, “Oh, amen.” (Laughter and applause) 
On the day of victory, all victories will be celebrated by saints, sages, and all your ancestors who are good. Nowadays, what is it? What is it, some disco? What is it? Disco or something? Nowadays, dancing is called disco, kissco, or something like that? But we dance beyond that, beyond that. (Dancing. Laughter) So while dancing, God falls down, and everyone falls down. After sleeping well, everyone has become a honey pot. (Laughter and applause) It’s so enjoyable that even looking at it is good, everyone is excited, and everything is sweet. 
So because it is so good and so strong, you forget to sleep, forget to work, and live intoxicated by that; that is the ideal. (Laughs) Do you want to go? “Yes.” Before going, do you want to die and live? “No.” Then I hope you become wonderful people returning home. Those who will do so, raise your hands. (Cheers) Is home church good or bad? Raise your hands and answer, raise your hands. “It’s good.” It’s really good. Amen! “Amen.” (Applause) *
